[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure thing! Here is a potential stress at work questionnaire:
```vbnet
1) How often do you feel stressed while working? (Always, Often, Sometimes, Rarely, Never)
2) On a scale of 0-10, how would rate your overall level of job satisfaction right now? Please explain why.
3) Do you have enough time to complete all the tasks assigned by management in one day or not and if no then what is causing this issue ? (Yes/No). If yes please elaborate on quality as well . 
4) How do you feel about your work-life balance right now? Are there any factors that are making it difficult for you to maintain a healthy lifestyle outside of the office environment. Please specify them if possible!  
5) Do you have enough resources and tools at workplace which can help in reducing stress levels ? (Yes/No). If no then please elaborate on what is missing . 
6) How do your colleagues behave towards each other? Is there a positive work culture or not, explain with reasons. Please specify if any particular person behaving negatively to you and why it's causing extra pressure for example bullying etc!  
7) Do management communicate effectively about changes in the company that might affect employees directly ? (Yes/No). If no then please elaborate on what can be done better so people feel more informed. 
8 ) Is there any particular task or project which is giving you stress and why? Please specify if possible!  
9) How do your physical working conditions impact the level of work-related pressure, for example lack of privacy , poor lighting etc ? (Yes/No). If no then please elaborate on what can be done better so people feel more comfortable. 
10 ) Do you have enough support from managers and supervisors when it comes to dealing with difficult tasks or not? Please specify if possible!  
```
And here is the same questionnaire in a conversational format:
- How often do you experience stress at work, on scale of always - never ? 2) Can we talk about your overall job satisfaction and what could be improved to make it better. For example , are there any factors that might affect employees directly which management should communicate more effectively .  3 ) Is the amount of time given for tasks enough or do you feel rushed, if not then how is quality being maintained ? 4) How would rate your work-life balance and what things outside office environment make it difficult to maintain a healthy lifestyle. Please specify them so we can find solution together !
5). Do think that resources provided at workplace are sufficient for reducing stress levels or do you feel something essential missing which might help in feeling more comfortable ? 6) Can tell me about your colleagues and work culture, is there positivity around to make things better? If not then who could be causing extra pressure by negative behavior.
7). Is management communicating effectively when it comes changes that can affect employees directly or do you feel left out of loop which might cause anxiety ? 8) Can we talk about any specific tasks giving stress and why, for example lack privacy , poor lighting etc . Let's find solution together !  9 ) Do think managers are providing enough support while dealing with difficult task? If not then who can help in making things better.
10). Finally let us discuss physical working conditions impacting level of work-related pressure and how we could improve them for example lack privacy , poor lighting etc . Let's find solution together !

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure thing! Here is a potential questionnaire about workplace environment:

1. How would you describe the physical working space? Is it comfortable, well-lit, and spacious enough for everyone's needs? Please rate from 0 (not at all) to 5(very much). If possible please provide specific examples in your answer! Thank You :) [2 - Comfortable]
2. How would you describe the temperature of this workplace environment on a scale of 1-7, with one being too cold and seven being very hot? Please share if it is easy to control or not as well (Yes/No)? If yes please rate how long does take for someone who has never used that system before.
3. How noisy are the machines in your workplace environment on a scale of 1-7, with one meaning almost silent and seven being very loud? Please share if it is easy to reduce noise or not (Yes/No)? If yes please rate how long does take for someone who has never used that system before
4. How would you describe the cleanliness in your workplace environment on a scale of 1-7, with one meaning almost no cleaning and seven being very high level? Please share if it is easy to maintain or not (Yes/No)? If yes please rate how long does take for someone who has never used that system before
5. How would you describe the air quality in your workplace environment on a scale of 1-7, with one meaning almost no freshness and seven being very high level? Please share if it is easy to maintain or not (Yes/No)? If yes please rate how long does take for someone who has never used that system before
6. How would you describe the availability of resources in your workplace environment on a scale of 1-7, with one meaning almost no and seven being very high level? Please share if it is easy to maintain or not (Yes/No)? If yes please rate how long does take for someone who has never used that system before
7. How would you describe the overall design in your workplace environment on a scale of 1-5, with one meaning almost no and five being very high level? Please share if it is easy to maintain or not (Yes/No)? If yes please rate how long does take for someone who has never used that system before
8. How would you describe the ergonomics in your workplace environment on a scale of 1-5, with one meaning almost no and five being very high level? Please share if it is easy to maintain or not (Yes/No)? If yes please rate how long does take for someone who has never used that system before
9. How would you describe the accessibility in your workplace environment on a scale of 1-5, with one meaning almost no and five being very high level? Please share if it is easy to maintain or not (Yes/No)? If yes please rate how long does take for someone who has never used that system before
10. How would you describe the overall atmosphere in your workplace environment on a scale of 1-5, with one meaning almost no and five being very high level? Please share if it is easy to maintain or not (Yes/No)? If yes please rate how long does take for someone who has never used that system before

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1173002
     - Topic: End of working relationship
     - Question number: 10
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.
Firstly, the user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic.
Then, the user will ask to convert it into a specified format.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. 

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on End of working relationship

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure thing! Here is a potential questionnaire for investigating end-of-working relationships:
1. Can you tell us about how many people in this company have experienced an involuntary termination? If so, what was the reason behind it and were they given any support to help them move on from that situation or not provided with enough time before their job responsibilities changed drastically due to downsizing/restructuring etc.
2. How does management team handle such situations when someone is let go because of poor performance, lack of skills required for new tasks and if there are any resources available like counseling services offered by HR department or not? Please elaborate on this topic as much detail possible so we can understand better what steps should be taken in future cases.
3. Is it true that certain employees get preferential treatment during layoffs, while others who may have been just as valuable (if not more) are left without a job and any kind of support system to fall back on? If yes then why is this happening because everyone deserves fairness regardless whether they're high up or lower in the hierarchy.
4. What measures has management taken over time, if at all, for making sure that people who leave company due involuntary reasons don’t feel like their contributions were not appreciated and how can we improve on those areas moving forward? Please share some examples here so our team knows what needs to be done proactively instead of waiting until something goes wrong.
5. How does HR communicate with employees about end-of working relationship, whether it's through an exit interview or other means like group meetings where everyone can hear how things went down and why certain decisions were made? Is there a consistent message being sent out by leadership team regarding this sensitive topic so all feel informed equally well in advance.
6. Can you provide us with data about the number of people who have left company voluntarily versus involuntary reasons, including those that might've been laid off due to budget constraints or other factors beyond their control? We want as much information here since this will help shape our policies going forward and ensure everyone feels supported regardless whether they stay long term.
7. How does management team measure employee satisfaction when someone is let go involuntarily, including those who might've been given opportunities to work remotely or have flexible hours but still felt like their contributions weren’t fully recognized by superiors? This question will help us understand if there are any gaps in our current approach and how we can fill them.
8. Finally, what steps has management taken over time for making sure that people who leave company due involuntary reasons don't feel left behind or forgotten once they no longer work here; please give examples so everyone understands the importance of this issue moving forward too!
     - User:

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire on training effectiveness:
```vbnet
1) How would you rate the overall quality of our employee training programs? (5-point scale, with strongly disagree being lowest score and strongly agree highest.) 
2) Have your employees been able to apply new skills learned in their day-to-day work after participating in a specific program or event?(Yes/No question. If yes please specify which skill(s))  
3) Do you think that the training programs offered are relevant for employee growth and development? (5 point scale, with strongly disagree being lowest score and Strongly agree highest.) 	
4) Have your employees been able to perform their jobs better after participating in a specific program or event?(Yes/No question. If yes please specify which job(s))  
5) Do you think that the training programs offered are accessible for all of our team members? (5 point scale, with strongly disagree being lowest score and Strongly agree highest.) 	
6) Have your employees been able to work more efficiently after participating in a specific program or event?(Yes/No question. If yes please specify which employee(s))  
7) Do you think that the training programs offered are engaging for our team members? (5 point scale, with strongly disagree being lowest score and Strongly agree highest.) 	
8 ) How many employees have participated in a specific program or event?(Number question. If unsure please specify range of participants).  
9) Have you noticed any change on the job performance level after training sessions were completed? (5 point scale, with strongly disagree being lowest score and Strongly agree highest.) 	
10 ) Do your employees feel comfortable asking questions or seeking help during a specific program/event if they don't understand something?(Yes / No question)  
```
Please let me know which format you would like this converted into. I can convert it to text, HTML and other formats as well!

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure thing! Here is a potential training-focused questionnaire for you:
```vbnet
1) How would you rate the overall effectiveness of our current employee training program? (Very satisfied, Somewhat Satisfied, Not sure, or Unsatisfied?) 
2a. Which specific trainings do your employees find most valuable and why?  	(Multiple choice: Technical Skills Training; Leadership/Management Development Programs ; Sales Techniques etc.)   
3) How often are new hires given the opportunity to attend training sessions within their first year of employment with us ? (Always, Sometimes or Never?) 
4. Do you think that our current trainings meet your business needs? If not which areas need improvement and why do they seem inadequate at this time?(Yes/No)  	If no: Please specify the area(s).   
5a How many employees have been able to attend training sessions within their first year of employment with us ? (Percentage or number?) 
6. What is your opinion on our current trainers? Are they knowledgeable and engaging enough for learners?(Yes/No) If no, what qualities do you think are essential in a trainer at this company that would make them more effective than the ones we currently have working with us ? Please specify  	 
7. How many employees prefer online training sessions over traditional classroom-style learning? (Percentage or number?)   
8a What is your opinion on our current eLearning courses and their design, if you've had a chance to evaluate them?(Yes/No) If no: Please specify the areas that need improvement.  	 
9 How do we ensure employees have access to training materials after they complete sessions? (Checklist or Multiple choice?)   
10a Do your current employee(s)/team members feel like their skills are being upgraded and meeting industry standards with our trainings?(Yes/No) If no, what areas need improvement ? Please specify.  	 
```
And here is the same questionnaire in a more conversational format:
1. How do you rate the overall effectiveness of your employee training program? Is there room for improvement or are employees generally satisfied with it?(Very Satisfied/Somewhat Satisifed, Not sure / Unsatisfied?) 
2a) Which specific trainings have been most valuable to both yourself and other team members in terms of meeting business needs ? (Multiple choice: Technical Skills Training; Leadership Development Programs ; Sales Techniques etc.)   
3. How often are new hires given the opportunity for professional development within their first year with us? Do they get enough chances or not?(Always, Sometimes / Never?) 
4) Are our current trainings able to meet your business needs and those of other employees ? If no which areas need improvement at this time.(Yes/No). Please specify if necessary.   
5a How many new hires have been trained within their first year with us? (Percentage or number?) 
6) What do you think about our current trainers in terms knowledge and engagement for learners ? Are they effective enough?( Yes / No ) If no, what qualities would make them more suitable at this company that could lead to better results. Please specify  	   
7). How many employees prefer online training sessions over traditional classroom-style learning? (Percentage or number?) 
8a) Have you had a chance yet to evaluate our eLearning courses and their design ? If not, what qualities do we need in order for them be considered effective by learners?(Yes/No). Please specify if necessary.   
9 ) How is accessibility of training materials ensured after employees complete sessions? (Checklist or Multiple choice?) 	  
10) Do your current employee(s)/team members feel like their skills are being upgraded and meeting industry standards with our trainings?(Yes/No). Please specify if necessary.

1. How would you rate this course overall, using stars as the rating system? (5-star being excellent and 0-star poor) Please provide your star count now...and any additional comments about what worked well in particular! * \* <https://www.amazon.com/dp/ASIN/>
2. How clear were you able to understand this course's content, including the language used by instructors and materials provided? (5-star being very easy for everyone) Please provide your star count now...and any additional comments about what worked well in particular! * \* <https://www.amazon.com/dp/ASIN/>
3. How would you rate this course's content, including the relevance of topics and materials provided? (5-star being very relevant) Please provide your star count now...and any additional comments about what worked well in particular! * \* <https://www.amazon.com/dp> /ASIN/>
4. How would you rate this course's instructors, including their knowledge and ability to explain concepts? (5-star being very good) Please provide your star count now...and any additional comments about what worked well in particular! * \* <https://www>.amazon<wink aspx> /dp/ASIN/>
5. How would you rate the course's pacing, including whether it was too fast or slow? (3-star being just right) Please provide your star count now...and any additional comments about what worked well in particular! * <https://www>.amazon<wink aspx> /dp/ASIN/>
6. How would you rate the course's materials, including whether they were useful and easy to understand? (5-star being very good) Please provide your star count now...and any additional comments about what worked well in particular! * <https://www>.amazon<wink aspx> /dp/ASIN/>
7. How would you rate the course's technology, including whether it was easy to use and navigate? (5-star being very good) Please provide your star count now...and any additional comments about what worked well in particular! * <https://www>.amazon<wink aspx> /dp/ASIN/>
8. How would you rate the course's ability to hold attention, including whether it was engaging and interactive? (5-star being very good) Please provide your star count now...and any additional comments about what worked well in particular! * <https://www>.amazon<wink aspx> /dp/ASIN/>
9. How would you rate the course's assessment methods, including whether they were fair and effective? (5-star being very good) Please provide your star count now...and any additional comments about what worked well in particular! * <https://www>.amazon<wink aspx> /dp/ASIN/>
10. How likely are you to recommend this course or training program, using stars again? (5-star being very much) Please provide your star count now...and any additional comments about what worked well in particular! * <https://www>.amazon<wink aspx> /dp/ASIN/>
Please note that these questions are just a starting point and can be modified to fit the specific needs of an organization. The goal is always for participants' feedback, so they feel heard by their instructors or organizers while providing valuable insights into what worked well in particular!

This JSON representation includes the following questions:

* Overall rating of the course (5-star being excellent and 0-star poor)
* Understanding of the course content (5-star being very easy for everyone)

 Sure! Here is a potential employee experience survey:
```vbnet
1) To what extent do you agree with this statement? "I feel like I am able to be myself at work." Strongly disagree / Somewhat disagree / Neutral / Slightly Agree / Completely Agree. Please explain your answer in a few sentences if possible! (Strong/Medium)
2) How often do you have the opportunity for open and honest communication with colleagues? Never, Rarely, Sometimes, Often or Always 	(Never-Always Scale). If not never then please give an example of when this has happened.  
3) Do your values match those espoused by our organization (either in terms of diversity/equity OR social justice)? Yes / No and if no why?   
4) How often do you feel like the work that needs to be done is too much for one person alone or does it seem overwhelming. Never, Rarely, Sometimes, Often or Always 	(Never-Always Scale). If not never then please give an example of when this has happened and how management could have made things better!   
5) How often do you feel like your work is meaningful? Almost always / Usually/ Occasionally. Please provide a specific instance where it was NOT to help us understand why that might be the case 	(Never-Always Scale).  
6) Do people in our organization seem authentic and genuine, or are they putting on an act for some reason (either because of social norms OR other factors)? Yes / No. If no then please explain who is not being real!   
7) How often do you feel like your work environment supports personal growth? Never/ Rarely/ Sometimes 	(Never-Always Scale). Please give an example if possible to help us understand how we can improve this situation for our employees and make it more commonplace.  
8 ) Do people in the organization seem committed or engaged with their jobs, either because they like them OR are passionate about what needs doing? Yes / No 	(Never-Always Scale). If not then please explain who is NOT!   
9) How often do you feel that your work environment supports personal growth and development for all employees (either through training or other means)? Never/ Rarely. Please give an example if possible to help us understand how we can improve this situation 	(Never-Always Scale).  
10 ) Do people in the organization seem like they are treated fairly, either by management OR colleagues? Yes / No and please explain who is not being fair!   
```
Please let me know if you would prefer a different format or need any changes. I am happy to help with that too (Strong/Medium).

Generate me a questionnaire on Career development

-------------------

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential career development questionnaire:

1. How do you define "career development"? Is it something that happens naturally, or does it require intentional effort?
2. What specific steps have you taken to further your own career development and advancement within the company? Can you share some examples of what has worked well for you in this regard?
3. How do you assess whether a particular opportunity is beneficial for someone's long-term growth, or just something that will help them get by day-to-day without any real progress being made towards their goals and aspirations over time (i.e., not all opportunities are created equal)? Please provide specific examples if possible!
4. In terms of career development: How do you feel about taking risks? Are they necessary in order to achieve certain things, or can a person reach the same destination through more traditional means without having taken any big leaps along their journey at work and life overall (i.e., is there an optimal level/balance between risk-taking vs safety)?
5. How do you measure success when it comes down specifically to career development? Is this something that can be quantified objectively, or does everyone have different criteria based on individual preferences & values systems in place at work and life overall (i.e., what specific metrics would qualify as "success" for someone)?
6. Can people really change their careers over time if they want to - i. e , is it possible that a person who has been working within one industry could transition into another field entirely without too much trouble, or does this take significant effort and planning ahead of time? Please share any experiences you might have had with others making such transitions successfully!
7. How do people's values impact their career development - i . e , if someone places a high value on something like family life over work-related successes & accolades, will they still be able to achieve professional growth and advancement within the company even though this might not align with what is traditionally considered "success"?
8. How do you know when it's time for career development? Is there a specific trigger or set of triggers that indicate someone should start thinking about moving up in their organization, rather than just staying put where they are currently at (i . e., how can we identify those who might be ripe and ready to take on new challenges)?
9. How do you feel about mentoring others within the company? Is this something everyone needs regardless of whether or not it's part of their job description, OR is more like an extra-curricular activity that only certain people should engage in if they have time/resources available to them (i . e., what are your thoughts on employee development and growth)?
10. Finally: How do you feel about the concept of "career ladders" - i.e, having clear paths laid out for employees so that everyone knows exactly how long it will take before they can reach certain milestones along their way at work? Or would such rigidity stifle creativity and innovation within your organization instead (i . e., what are the pros & cons of career ladders)?
Please let me know if you need any further information or clarification!

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire for investigating career path clarity within an organization:
1) How would you describe the level of transparency around different job roles in this company? Is it easy to understand how they fit into broader organizational goals and what skills are required at each stage?
2) Do employees feel that there is a clear progression from one role or career pathway to another, with defined steps for growth within their current position as well as future opportunities available through promotion paths (e.g., manager/senior specialist)? If not, why do you think this might be the case?
3) Is it possible for employees in your company who are interested and motivated about a particular role or career pathway to access resources such as mentoring programs that will help them achieve those goals without feeling like they're being held back by lack of support from management team members, etc. ? 4) How often do you communicate with staff regarding their specific roles/career paths within the company and how these align generally towards organizational objectives? Is there a sense among employees that this communication is regular enough or not at all
5) Are career pathways clearly defined for every role in your organization, including those who may be considered "lower level" positions but still important to overall success of business operations. If so - how do you ensure these paths are accessible and understood by everyone? 6) Is there a culture within the company where employees feel comfortable discussing their career aspirations with managers/supervisors without fearing negative consequences or judgement, thus allowing them an opportunity for growth & development through open communication channels
7) Do new hires receive information about potential future roles and how they can progress into those positions once employed by your organization. If not - why is this important to communicate early on in employee journey? 8 ) Is there a sense of fairness when it comes down promoting people based upon merit rather than just seniority, thus creating more equitable environment where everyone has equal chance regardless position within company hierarchy
9) How do you measure success rate for internal promotions and how often is this measured. This will help understand if current system needs improvement or not 10 ) Is there any specific training provided to employees who are about be promoted, so they can hit ground running with new role & responsibilities? If yes - what kind of trainings do you provide
Please let me know which format would like this converted into. Thank You!

Generate me a questionnaire on Career Path Clarity

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire for investigating career path clarity within an organization:
1) How would you describe the level of transparency around different job roles in this company? Is it easy to understand how they fit into broader organizational goals and what skills are required at each stage?
2) Do employees feel that there is a clear progression from one role or career pathway to another, with defined steps for growth within their current position as well as future opportunities available through promotion paths (e.g., manager/senior specialist)? If not, why do you think this might be the case?
3) Is it possible for employees in your company who are interested and motivated about a particular role or career pathway to access resources such as mentoring programs that will help them achieve those goals without feeling like they're being held back by lack of support from management team members, etc. ? 4) How often do you communicate with staff regarding their specific roles/career paths within the company and how these align generally towards organizational objectives? Is there a sense among employees that this communication is regular enough or not at all
5) Are career pathways clearly defined for every role in your organization, including those who may be considered "lower level" positions but still important to overall success of business operations. If so - how do you ensure these paths are accessible and understood by everyone? 6) Is there a culture within the company where employees feel comfortable discussing their career aspirations with managers/supervisors without fearing negative consequences or judgement, thus allowing them an opportunity for growth & development through open communication channels
7) Do new hires receive information about potential future roles and how they can progress into those positions once employed by your organization. If not - why is this important to communicate early on in employee journey? 8 ) Is there a sense of fairness when it comes down promoting people based upon merit rather than just seniority, thus creating more equitable environment where everyone has equal chance regardless position within company hierarchy
9) How do you measure success rate for internal promotions and how often is this measured. This will help understand if current system needs improvement or not 10 ) Is there any specific training provided to employees who are about be promoted, so they can hit ground running with new role & responsibilities? If yes - what kind of trainings do you provide
Please let me know which format would like this converted into. Thank You!

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential kick-off meeting feedback questionnaire:
```vbnet
1) On a scale of 0 - 10, how would you rate the overall effectiveness of this kick off meeting? Please explain your answer.
2) Did all necessary stakeholders attend and participate in the discussion? If not, who was missing and why do they think it is important for them to be involved next time?
3) Was there a clear agenda with specific goals outlined beforehand or did you feel that topics were being discussed randomly without any particular purpose? Please specify. 
4) Did attendees have the opportunity to provide input on meeting objectives and structure, as well as contribute ideas about how things should be done in future meetings of this kind ? If not, why do they think it is important for people's voices to be heard next time around too so that everyone feels included?
5) How would you rate your satisfaction with the level of collaboration between team members during today’ s kick off meeting. Were there any communication barriers or misunderstandings due lack either in terms language, cultural differences etc.. Please elaborate 6 ) In order to make sure all participants can fully understand and contribute effectively within a given time frame , was enough attention paid towards pacing the session so that no one felt left behind?
7) How well do you think this kick off meeting helped establish an atmosphere of trust among team members, which is essential for productive collaboration going forward ? Please provide specific examples if possible. 8 ) Were any visual aids or other materials used during today’s Kick Off Meeting that could have been more effective in terms engaging participants and helping them understand concepts better?  Sure! I can help with that. Here is a potential questionnaire for investigating the ONBOARDING EXPERIENCE at a company:
```
1. How would you describe the overall atmosphere and culture of your organization during an employee's first few days? Is it welcoming, or do new hires feel like they have to earn their place in the team through hard work alone? Please rate this on a scale from 0-5 (with five being most positive).
2. Were you provided with all necessary resources and materials during your ONBOARDING process at our company? If not, which ones were missing or difficult for new hires to access due to lack of information/technology support etcetera ? Please specify if possible so we can improve this experience in future! (0=No; 1-2 = Somewhat but could be better ;3=Yes)
3. How long did it take you before feeling comfortable with your colleagues and superiors? Did they make an effort to get know more about YOU as person, or was there a sense of distance between everyone else except management team members who might have been too busy dealing day-to–day tasks ? Please rate this on scale 0 -5 (with five being most positive).
4. Were you given clear instructions regarding your role and responsibilities? How easy/difficult did it feel for understanding what exactly is expected from YOU in terms of performance, goals etcetera . Rate please using following options: Very Easy – Somewhat difficult but manageable - Difficult; Impossible (0=No ; 1-2 =Somehow not clear enough)
5. How well do you think our company has integrated new hires into existing teams and projects? Were there any challenges that made it harder for someone to become part of the team, or was this process smooth sailing all along ? Please rate using scale from0 - 3 (with three being most positive). Thank You!
6. How would you describe communication channels within our organization during your onboarding period? Were they open and transparent enough so new hires could feel free to ask questions without feeling intimidated by hierarchy or other factors impacting their ability/willingness ? Please rate using following options: Very Open & Transparent – Somewhat but with some room for improvement - Closed; Not at all (0=No ; 1-2 =Somehow not clear enough)
7. How much time did you get to spend face–to--face or one on ones, rather than just through emails and calls? Do YOU think this was sufficient in order fully understand company's vision mission values etcetera ? Please rate using scale from 0 -5 (with five being most positive).
8. Finally , do we provide enough support during first few days/weeks after starting job, both technically as well emotionally if necessary? This could include things like orientation sessions or mentoring program where new hires can learn more about company culture and expectations in relaxed manner . Please rate using scale from 0 -5 (with five being most positive).
Please let me know whether you need any further assistance. Thank You!

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire for investigating work-life balance within a company:
1. How do you feel about the amount of time you spend working versus engaging in personal activities? Is it evenly balanced, or are there certain days when one activity takes precedence over another?
2. Do you think that your employer values and respects your life outside work as much they should be doing so for a healthy balance between professional and private lives to exist? Please elaborate on the reasons behind this answer if possible! (For example, do other commitments make it difficult?) 3a) How often does stress from job spill over into personal time or activities because of its intensity/volume at work hours; If yes then how can we reduce that so you feel more comfortable?
4. Is there any pressure on employees to be available beyond their scheduled working day, which might negatively impact mental health and relationships outside the office environment (either from management level directly OR indirectly through team members)? 5a) Do people have enough time off during weekends/vacations if needed? Or do they feel guilty about taking those breaks due to workload or pressure related with deadlines etc.
6b). In terms of communication, how would you rate the company's efforts in making sure everyone can maintain a healthy balance between their personal and professional lives without feeling overwhelmed by either one too much - on scale 1-5 (where five means excellent)? Please provide specific examples if possible!
7c) How many hours do people usually work per week, including overtime? Is this sustainable for them in long term or not really considering health aspects as well other factors involved like family life etc. Also mention whether they feel encouraged to take regular breaks during working day/hours and reasons behind that if known!
8d) Does management team within organization understand importance of work-life balance, especially when it comes down managing people who might need more flexibility due personal circumstances? If not then how can we make sure this message gets across clearly without causing tension between staff members. 9e). Finally - do you think that your company provides enough support and resources for employees to maintain a healthy lifestyle both at work AND outside of office hours, including mental health awareness programs or similar initiatives aimed towards well-being? If not then what could be done differently in order make this happen more effectively!
Please let me know if there are any specific formats you would like these questions converted into. I'm here to help and ensure that your questionnaire is as effective, engaging, and insightful as possible for the people who complete it - thank you!"

 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire for investigating work-life balance within a company:
1. How do you feel about the amount of time you spend working versus engaging in personal activities? Is it evenly balanced, or are there certain days when one activity takes precedence over another?
2. Do you think that your employer values and respects your life outside work as much they should be doing so for a healthy balance between professional and private lives to exist? Please elaborate on the reasons behind this answer if possible! (For example, do other commitments make it difficult?) 3a) How often does stress from job spill over into personal time or activities because of its intensity/volume at work hours; If yes then how can we reduce that so you feel more comfortable?
4. Is there any pressure on employees to be available beyond their scheduled working day, which might negatively impact mental health and relationships outside the office environment (either from management level directly OR indirectly through team members)? 5a) Do people have enough time off during weekends/vacations if needed? Or do they feel guilty about taking those breaks due to workload or pressure related with deadlines etc.
6b). In terms of communication, how would you rate the company's efforts in making sure everyone can maintain a healthy balance between their personal and professional lives without feeling overwhelmed by either one too much - on scale 1-5 (where five means excellent)? Please provide specific examples if possible!
7c) How many hours do people usually work per week, including overtime? Is this sustainable for them in long term or not really considering health aspects as well other factors involved like family life etc. Also mention whether they feel encouraged to take regular breaks during working day/hours and reasons behind that if known!
8d) Does management team within organization understand importance of work-life balance, especially when it comes down managing people who might need more flexibility due personal circumstances? If not then how can we make sure this message gets across clearly without causing tension between staff members. 9e). Finally - do you think that your company provides enough support and resources for employees to maintain a healthy lifestyle both at work AND outside of office hours, including mental health awareness programs or similar initiatives aimed towards well-being?  Sure thing! Here is a potential questionnaire on workload management:

2. Have you ever felt overwhelmed with the amount of responsibilities given to handle during your working hours? If yes, what steps did you take then – were those effective for managing that situation better next time around too (if applicable)? 🎯
3. How do YOU define workload management and its importance in an organization/team setting vs individual settings where one person might be handling multiple tasks simultaneously without any support from others? Is there a difference between these two scenarios as per your understanding or experience so far, if yes then what are they (if applicable)? 🎯
4. In terms of workload management – do you think technology plays an important role in making things more organized and efficient OR is it just about people skills & time allocation which can make all the difference? Please elaborate with examples from your personal experience if possible! Thank You :).5 . Is there a process for this that ensures everyone has manageable workload while still pushing them enough so they feel challenged but not overwhelmed by any means necessary! 🎯7 . 8. How would YOU measure success when talking about workload management? Is there any specific metric(s) used in your organization, if yes then please share with us so we too can benefit from such wisdom here! 🎯9 . Have you ever felt that certain tasks are just not getting done because of high-volume intake and lack proper planning beforehand – this could include meetings or even small things like emails. If Yes - How did it affect your productivity, motivation levels etc., if no then great but still curious how do YOU keep track on these aspects daily (if applicable)?

You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.
Firstly, the user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Culture

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire about workplace culture:

1. How would you describe the overall atmosphere at work? Is it generally positive or negative? Please provide specific examples if possible.
2. Do people in your organization feel comfortable being themselves, and do they think their individuality is respected by others around them? Can employees be open with each other about personal matters without fear of judgment from colleagues/supervisors etc., OR does this only happen behind closed doors because it's "not safe" to share opinions openly at work place.
3. Is there a sense that everyone has an equal chance for success regardless of their background, or do certain people have more opportunities than others due solely based on who they are? Are all employees encouraged and given same resources needed so every one can reach full potential in organization OR is it just few select individuals getting special treatment while rest struggle with limited means.
4. How well does your company's values align with those of its staff members, both personally AND professionally speaking ? Is there a strong connection between personal beliefs and organizational mission/goals or not really? And if yes then how this is measured & reinforced within the organization so that everyone feels included in it rather than just being part because they need paycheck.
5. How often do you feel like your ideas are heard, considered AND implemented at work place ? Or does management only listen when something goes wrong and quick fixes needed without much thought given to long term consequences of decisions taken hastily under pressure from outside sources (like customers/clients etc.) . Also whether people can speak freely about what they think should be done differently in order for organization's success, or do some voices get silenced while others dominate conversation.
6. Is there a feeling that everyone is treated fairly and consistently within the company? Or does favoritism play role where certain individuals always seem to receive preferential treatment over other equally qualified candidates simply because they are "favorites" of those in power positions, even though this might not be true for all cases but only few specific ones.
7. How well do people understand their roles and responsibilities within the organization? Are there clear guidelines about what is expected from each employee so everyone knows exactly where stand when it comes to performance evaluations/feedback sessions etc., OR does confusion exist around certain tasks which leads some individuals feeling overwhelmed while others enjoy more freedom due lack of clarity.
8. How often do you feel like your work environment encourages creativity and innovation, or is there a strict adherence to rules with little room for deviation from established protocols? Is it possible within the organization's current structure/culture that new ideas can be introduced easily without causing too much disruption in flow of things OR does this require special permission which may not always granted.
9. How often do you feel like your company cares about its employees as people, rather than just resources? Is there a sense within the organization where everyone feels valued and respected regardless if they're janitor or CEO level person working at same place ? Can all members of workforce expect equal treatment irrespective rank/position OR does some get preferential care over others.
10. Finally, how well do you think your company listens to its employees? Is there a mechanism in the organization where everyone can share their thoughts and opinions openly without fearing negative consequences or backlash from management team etc., Or is it just few select individuals who have this privilege while rest struggle with being heard due power dynamics.
Please let me know if you would like any changes made to these questions!

Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Culture

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire about workplace culture:

1. How would you describe the overall atmosphere at work? Is it generally positive or negative? Please provide specific examples if possible.
2. Do people in your organization feel comfortable being themselves, and do they think their individuality is respected by others around them? Can employees be open with each other about personal matters without fear of judgment from colleagues/supervisors etc., OR does this only happen behind closed doors because it's "not safe" to share opinions openly at work place.
3. Is there a sense that everyone has an equal chance for success regardless of their background, or do certain people have more opportunities than others due solely based on who they are? Are all employees encouraged and given same resources needed so every one can reach full potential in organization OR is it just few select individuals getting special treatment while rest struggle with limited means.
4. How well does your company's values align with those of its staff members, both personally AND professionally speaking ? Is there a strong connection between personal beliefs and organizational mission/goals or not really? And if yes then how this is measured & reinforced within the organization so that everyone feels included in it rather than just being part because they need paycheck.
5. How often do you feel like your ideas are heard, considered AND implemented at work place ? Or does management only listen when something goes wrong and quick fixes needed without much thought given to long term consequences of decisions taken hastily under pressure from outside sources (like customers/clients etc.) . Also whether people can speak freely about what they think should be done differently in order for organization's success, or do some voices get silenced while others dominate conversation.
6. Is there a feeling that everyone is treated fairly and consistently within the company? Or does favoritism play role where certain individuals always seem to receive preferential treatment over other equally qualified candidates simply because they are "favorites" of those in power positions, even though this might not be true for all cases but only few specific ones.
7. How well do people understand their roles and responsibilities within the organization? Are there clear guidelines about what is expected from each employee so everyone knows exactly where stand when it comes to performance evaluations/feedback sessions etc., OR does confusion exist around certain tasks which leads some individuals feeling overwhelmed while others enjoy more freedom due lack of clarity.
8. How often do you feel like your work environment encourages creativity and innovation, or is there a strict adherence to rules with little room for deviation from established protocols? Is it possible within the organization's current structure/culture that new ideas can be introduced easily without causing too much disruption in flow of things OR does this require special permission which may not always granted.
9. How often do you feel like your company cares about its employees as people, rather than just resources? Is there a sense within the organization where everyone feels valued and respected regardless if they're janitor or CEO level person working at same place ? Can all members of workforce expect equal treatment irrespective rank/position OR does some get preferential care over others.
10. Finally, how well do you think your company listens to its employees? Is there a mechanism in the organization where everyone can share their thoughts and opinions openly without fearing negative consequences or backlash from management team etc., Or is it just few select individuals who have this privilege while rest struggle with being heard due power dynamics.
Please let me know if you would like any changes made to these questions!
